 ‚Äô The International Cricket Council (ICC) approved a proposal to change its structure for better governance, which would make India's role in the International Cricket Council's control of revenue and rights more important
 bhartiya cricket control board (bisisiai) ke adhyaksh en
 Srinivasan will take over as the chairman of the ICC Board from July
 pakistan, srilanka or dakshin africa ke kade virodh ke baavjood isisi ke dhaanche main badlaav ke vivaadit prastaav ko kaaryakari board kii baithak main manjuuri de di gai
 It received the support of eight of the ten full-time members of the ICC, while Pakistan and Sri Lanka did not attend the meeting
 is prastaav ke pramukh binduon main kaaryakari samiti or vitt tathaa vanijyik maamalon kii samiti kaa gathan shaamil he
 The statement said that both the BCCI, CA and ECB will remain on the sub-committees while two other representatives will be among the full-time members to be elected by the board
 isisi ne ek bayaan main kaha ki ek nai kaaryakari samiti kaa gathan kiya jayega, jo board ko report karegi
 The first Chairman of the Executive Committee will be Wally Edwards of Cricket Australia, while the Chairman of the Finance and Commercial Affairs Committee will remain Giles Clarke of the ECB
 ye donon pehle do saal tak adhyaksh rahenge
 After the completion of this phase of change, the Chairman of the ICC Board will be selected from the ICC Board and all full-time member directors will have the right to stand for election
 ab sambandhit prastaavon ko unase judi samitiyon or board ke paas bheja jayega or phir manjuuri ke liye parishad ke saamne rakhaa jayega
 Other important points in the proposal include the formation of a Test Cricket Fund to preserve the traditional format of the game, in which associate members will get a chance to play the test, creating a new financial model for full-time members
 isisi ne yah bhi kaha ki sabhi purnakalik sadasyon ne isaki pushti kii he ki ve jaldi hi dwipaksheeya shrinkhalaaon ke liye qaraar karenge taaki future tours kaarykram kaa vyapak shedul banaaya ja sake, jo ab 2023 tak ke liye hoga
 The ICC has also decided to hold the Champions Trophy in 2017 and 2021 instead of the World Test Championship
 bayaan main kaha gaya he ki test cricket main chaar tiimon ke finels vaala praaroop taiyaar kar paanaa sambhav nahin tha, jo test cricket kii aatma ko barkaraar rakh sake
 It said that the ICC Champions Trophy, ICC Cricket World Cup and ICC T20 World Cup Venues have been decided, so from 2015 to 2023 the ICC has an attractive package
 prastaav main pramukh associat sadasyon ko sahyog badhaane kii bhi baat kahi gai he
 The ICC claims that funds directly to associate and affiliate countries will be increased
 unke liye toornamenton ke aayojanon ke alaava kai suvidhaayen bhi muhaiyaa karai jaaengi

 ICC President Alain Issac welcomed the decision, saying that the board has taken some important decisions today, which will give us long-term certainty about governance, competition and the icc's economic model
 unhone kaha ki yah faisla sadasyon ke bich lambii baatcheet ke baad liya gaya
